If polling mode doesn't work, it further switches to single_cmd mode (line 951). However, these flags (polling_mode and single_cmd) are never reset when the driver suspends and resumes.\n\nAfter a suspend/resume cycle, the hardware is reset and should be able to communicate normally again using the standard interrupt-based CORB/RIRB mode.
